28           /* transaction_date is used to segment data to load cube */
29           create table segments as
30             select distinct transaction_date from postgres.FACT_TRANSACTIONS order by transaction_date desc;
NOTE: Table WORK.SEGMENTS created, with 791 rows and 1 columns.

31           /* insert segments into macro list to interate through */
32           select transaction_date into :segment1 - :segment999999 from segments;
33           /* get the number of records for counter for loop */
34           select count(transaction_date) into :segment_count from segments;
35         quit;

309        
310        /*** Macro to iterate through remaining segments and load cube ***/
311        %macro LoadSegmentsIntoCube;
312        /* incrementally load cube by updating a view in each step then incrementally adding data to the cube */
313        %do x=2 %to &segment_count;
314          /* if no errors (warnings can exist) then proceed */
315          %if &syserr. eq 0 or &syserr. eq 4 %then %do;
316        
317            /* update segmented data */
318            %put ****** Load next segment into table to incrementally load cube for segment = &&segment&x ******;
319            proc sql threads;
320              create table SGF2013.FACT_TRANSACTIONS_SEGMENT as
321                select * from postgres.FACT_TRANSACTIONS
322                  where transaction_date = &&segment&x
323              ;
324            quit;
18                                                         The SAS System                          09:12 Saturday, December 15, 2012

325        
326            /* Incrementally update cube */
327            %put ****** LOAD cube for snapshot = &&segment&x ******;
328            proc olap
329              CUBE                   = "&cube"
330              DATA                   = SGF2013.FACT_TRANSACTIONS_SEGMENT
331              ADD_DATA
332              UPDATE_INPLACE
333              IGNORE_MISSING_DIMKEYS = VERBOSE
334              ;
335        
336            METASVR
337                HOST        = "vSAS"
338                PORT        = 8561
339                OLAP_SCHEMA = "SASApp - OLAP Schema";
340        
341              /*** IMPORTANT: Update this list if new dimensions are added ****/
342              DIMENSION Location UPDATE_DIMENSION = MEMBERS;
343              DIMENSION Time UPDATE_DIMENSION = MEMBERS;
344              DIMENSION 'Party Account'n UPDATE_DIMENSION = MEMBERS;
345              DIMENSION 'Transaction Type'n UPDATE_DIMENSION = MEMBERS;
346        
347            run;
348        
349            %put ******** Coalesce NWAY **********;
350            proc olap
351              CUBE                   = "&cube"
352               COALESCE_AGGREGATIONS;
353        
354              METASVR
355                  HOST        = "vSAS"
356                  PORT        = 8561
357                  OLAP_SCHEMA = "SASApp - OLAP Schema";
358        
359            run;
360        
361            %put ****** FINISH loading for snapshot = &&segment&x ******;
362          %end;
363          %else %do; /* if errors exist */
364            %put *********** ERRORS DETECTED: ABORTING **********;
365            %abort cancel;
366          %end;
367        
368        %end;
369        %mend LoadSegmentsIntoCube;
370        
371        /* disable log during macro */
372        options nosource;
